Title P.Herc. 229, 242, 243, 247, 248, 433, 437, 1077, 1088, 1098, 1428, 1609, 1610, 1648, 1788
Work Philodemus, De pietate
Content Philodemus; peri eusebeias (de pietate), with stichometry and title [1428]
